several layers in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository:\\n\\n## 1. Deprecation Warning Generation\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go`** is the core enforcement file. It defines:\\n- `IsDeprecated()` — checks if an API object implements `APILifecycleDeprecated()` and whether the current server version meets or exceeds the deprecation version.\\n- `WarningMessage()` — generates the human-readable deprecation warning string (e.g., 'extensions/v1beta1 Ingress is deprecated in v1.14+, unavailable in v1.22+; use networking.k8s.io/v1 Ingress').\\n- `RemovedRelease()` — returns the major.minor version in which the API will be/was removed.\\n- `MajorMinor()` — parses version info.\\n\\n## 2. Warning Injection into API Routes\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go`** is where the API route registration happens. It calls `deprecation.IsDeprecated()`, `deprecation.WarningMessage()`, and `deprecation.RemovedRelease()` for each registered API type, then calls `utilwarning.AddWarningsHandler()` to wrap each route handler with automatic warning emission.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go`** defines `AddWarningsHandler()` which wraps a route function to inject warnings via `warning.AddWarning()` on every request.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go`** defines the `Recorder` interface, `WithWarningRecorder()` to attach a recorder to the request context, and `AddWarning()` to record warnings.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go`** defines the HTTP middleware `WithWarningRecorder()` that attaches a deduplicating recorder to every request's context and writes RFC 7234 `Warning` response headers.\\n\\n## 3. Metrics and Audit Annotations\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go`** records the `requested_deprecated_apis` Prometheus gauge and sets audit annotations `k8s.io/deprecated=true` and `k8s.io/removed-release=<version>` on requests to deprecated API versions.\\n\\n## 4. Removal Version Enforcement\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go`** implements `resourceExpirationEvaluator` with:\\n- `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator()` — creates evaluator with current version\\n- `ShouldServeForVersion(majorRemoved, minorRemoved)` — returns false if the API's removal version is <= current server version (with alpha/beta exemptions and KUBE_APISERVER_SERVE_REMOVED_APIS_FOR_ONE_RELEASE escape hatch)\\n- `RemoveDeletedKinds()` — iterates all registered storage and removes any whose `APILifecycleRemoved()` indicates they should no longer be served\\n\\n**`pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go`** calls `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator` and `RemoveDeletedKinds` during API server startup to purge removed API versions from the API group storage map.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/kube-aggregator/pkg/apiserver/apiserver.go`** similarly calls `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator` for the aggregated API server.\\n\\n## 5. CRD Deprecation\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go`** handles deprecated CRD versions: it reads the `Deprecated` and `DeprecationWarning` fields from CRD version specs, and calls `warning.AddWarning()` for requests to deprecated CRD versions. The `defaultDeprecationWarning()` function generates a default deprecation message pointing to the next non-deprecated version.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go`** validates CRD deprecation settings via `validateDeprecationWarning()`, ensuring `DeprecationWarning` is only set on deprecated versions, is not empty, and is within character limits.\\n\\n## 6. Minimum Supported API Version (MinCompatibilityVersion)\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/version/version.go`** defines the `EffectiveVersion` interface with `MinCompatibilityVersion()` and its `Validate()` method which enforces that `minCompatibilityVersion` is within [binaryMinor-1] for alpha builds.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go`** uses `MinCompatibilityVersion()` in `emulatedStorageVersion()` to select the appropriate storage API version for backward compatibility, skipping API versions introduced after the min-compatibility version.\\n\\n**`cmd/kube-apiserver/app/options/validation.go`** calls `ValidateKubeEffectiveVersion()` at startup to enforce that emulation/compatibility version settings are valid.\\n\\n## 7. Lifecycle Code Generator\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/code-generator/cmd/prerelease-lifecycle-gen/prerelease-lifecycle-generators/status.go`** is the code generator that reads `// +k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:deprecated=X.Y`, `// +k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:removed=X.Y`, and `// +k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:introduced=X.Y` tags from API type comments and generates the `APILifecycleDeprecated()`, `APILifecycleRemoved()`, and `APILifecycleIntroduced()` methods into `zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go` files for each API version package.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":1,"cache_creation_input_tokens":375,"cache_read_input_tokens":54888,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":375,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":0},"output_tokens":18,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"641edba9-df5e-4c7f-9fc4-a8075abfa069","uuid":"c35fa0b9-59b1-411f-94b4-35d8aa807646"}

several layers in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository:\\n\\n## 1. Deprecation Warning Generation\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/deprecation/deprecation.go`** is the core enforcement file. It defines:\\n- `IsDeprecated()` — checks if an API object implements `APILifecycleDeprecated()` and whether the current server version meets or exceeds the deprecation version.\\n- `WarningMessage()` — generates the human-readable deprecation warning string (e.g., 'extensions/v1beta1 Ingress is deprecated in v1.14+, unavailable in v1.22+; use networking.k8s.io/v1 Ingress').\\n- `RemovedRelease()` — returns the major.minor version in which the API will be/was removed.\\n- `MajorMinor()` — parses version info.\\n\\n## 2. Warning Injection into API Routes\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/installer.go`** is where the API route registration happens. It calls `deprecation.IsDeprecated()`, `deprecation.WarningMessage()`, and `deprecation.RemovedRelease()` for each registered API type, then calls `utilwarning.AddWarningsHandler()` to wrap each route handler with automatic warning emission.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/warning/warning.go`** defines `AddWarningsHandler()` which wraps a route function to inject warnings via `warning.AddWarning()` on every request.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/warning/context.go`** defines the `Recorder` interface, `WithWarningRecorder()` to attach a recorder to the request context, and `AddWarning()` to record warnings.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/filters/warning.go`** defines the HTTP middleware `WithWarningRecorder()` that attaches a deduplicating recorder to every request's context and writes RFC 7234 `Warning` response headers.\\n\\n## 3. Metrics and Audit Annotations\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/endpoints/metrics/metrics.go`** records the `requested_deprecated_apis` Prometheus gauge and sets audit annotations `k8s.io/deprecated=true` and `k8s.io/removed-release=<version>` on requests to deprecated API versions.\\n\\n## 4. Removal Version Enforcement\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/deleted_kinds.go`** implements `resourceExpirationEvaluator` with:\\n- `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator()` — creates evaluator with current version\\n- `ShouldServeForVersion(majorRemoved, minorRemoved)` — returns false if the API's removal version is <= current server version (with alpha/beta exemptions and KUBE_APISERVER_SERVE_REMOVED_APIS_FOR_ONE_RELEASE escape hatch)\\n- `RemoveDeletedKinds()` — iterates all registered storage and removes any whose `APILifecycleRemoved()` indicates they should no longer be served\\n\\n**`pkg/controlplane/apiserver/apis.go`** calls `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator` and `RemoveDeletedKinds` during API server startup to purge removed API versions from the API group storage map.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/kube-aggregator/pkg/apiserver/apiserver.go`** similarly calls `NewResourceExpirationEvaluator` for the aggregated API server.\\n\\n## 5. CRD Deprecation\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apiserver/customresource_handler.go`** handles deprecated CRD versions: it reads the `Deprecated` and `DeprecationWarning` fields from CRD version specs, and calls `warning.AddWarning()` for requests to deprecated CRD versions. The `defaultDeprecationWarning()` function generates a default deprecation message pointing to the next non-deprecated version.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiextensions-apiserver/pkg/apis/apiextensions/validation/validation.go`** validates CRD deprecation settings via `validateDeprecationWarning()`, ensuring `DeprecationWarning` is only set on deprecated versions, is not empty, and is within character limits.\\n\\n## 6. Minimum Supported API Version (MinCompatibilityVersion)\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/component-base/version/version.go`** defines the `EffectiveVersion` interface with `MinCompatibilityVersion()` and its `Validate()` method which enforces that `minCompatibilityVersion` is within [binaryMinor-1] for alpha builds.\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/server/storage/resource_encoding_config.go`** uses `MinCompatibilityVersion()` in `emulatedStorageVersion()` to select the appropriate storage API version for backward compatibility, skipping API versions introduced after the min-compatibility version.\\n\\n**`cmd/kube-apiserver/app/options/validation.go`** calls `ValidateKubeEffectiveVersion()` at startup to enforce that emulation/compatibility version settings are valid.\\n\\n## 7. Lifecycle Code Generator\\n\\n**`staging/src/k8s.io/code-generator/cmd/prerelease-lifecycle-gen/prerelease-lifecycle-generators/status.go`** is the code generator that reads `// +k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:deprecated=X.Y`, `// +k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:removed=X.Y`, and `// +k8s:prerelease-lifecycle-gen:introduced=X.Y` tags from API type comments and generates the `APILifecycleDeprecated()`, `APILifecycleRemoved()`, and `APILifecycleIntroduced()` methods into `zz_generated.prerelease-lifecycle.go` files for each API version package.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
